                                                                 (static_cast<float>(Cursor.total_seen) / (
                                                                      TF_RAMP_SIZE * ExamplesPerEpoch)),
                                                                 0.f, 1.f) * 100.f;
                            std::snprintf(line, sizeof(line),
                                          "%s  g%d/%lu b%d/%zu  loss=%.3f  ss=%.2f  len=%d  ep=%.2f  ce_lr_pct_max_magnitude=%.2f%%",
                                          EpochBar(Cursor.total_seen).c_str(),
                                          g + 1, Groups, b + 1, n_batches,
                                          group_loss / static_cast<float>(b + 1), p_ss,
                                          cur_max_len,
                                          static_cast<float>(Cursor.total_seen) / ExamplesPerEpoch,
                                          ce_ramp_pct);
                            std::cout << line << "\n";
                        }

                        if (Cursor.total_seen / ExamplesPerEpoch > prev_total / ExamplesPerEpoch) {
                            const float running_training_loss = batches > 0
                                                                    ? loss_acc / static_cast<float>(batches)
                                                                    : group_loss / static_cast<float>(b + 1);
                            const float cur_rl_reward = rl_reward_count > 0
                                                            ? rl_reward_acc / static_cast<float>(rl_reward_count)
                                                            : -1.f;
                            const float cur_rl_acc = rl_reward_count > 0
                                                         ? rl_acc_acc / static_cast<float>(rl_reward_count)
                                                         : -1.f;

                            const long ep = Cursor.total_seen / ExamplesPerEpoch;
                            std::cout << "\n══════════ " << ep << " × "
                                    << ExamplesPerEpoch << " TRAINED ══════════\n";

                            DistResult tf_dist, ar_dist;
                            auto [tf_loss, ar_loss] = timed("[test]", [this, &tf_dist, &ar_dist, &ss_rng]() {
                                return EvalTestSet(tf_dist, ar_dist, ss_rng);
                            });
                            std::cout << "[test] tf_loss=" << tf_loss << "\n";
                            std::cout << "[test] ar_loss=" << ar_loss << "\n";

                            const float b_tf = (static_cast<float>(ExamplesPerEpoch) / Batch)
                                               * LR(Cursor.total_seen);
                            const float b_rl = static_cast<float>(rl_reward_count)
                                               * RL_State.LR(Cursor.total_seen);
                            const float b_tot = b_tf + b_rl;
                            std::cout << "[budget] tf=" << b_tf << " (" << 100.f * b_tf / b_tot << "%)"
                                      << "  rl=" << b_rl << " (" << 100.f * b_rl / b_tot << "%)\n";

                            WriteProgressJSON(progress_base + "_" + std::to_string(Cursor.total_seen) + ".json",
                                              Cursor.total_seen, Cursor.lap, running_training_loss, tf_loss,
                                              cur_rl_reward, cur_rl_acc, ar_loss, &tf_dist, &ar_dist,
                                              50, b_tf, b_rl);
                            Network.Save(progress_base + "_save_" + std::to_string(Cursor.total_seen) + ".bin");
                            Network.SaveForTraining(checkpoint_model);

                            std::cout << "[save] model + test-JSON @ trained=" << Cursor.total_seen << "\n";
                            RunDashboard();

                            loss_acc = 0.f;
                            batches = 0;
                            rl_reward_acc = 0.f;
                            rl_acc_acc = 0.f;
                            rl_reward_count = 0;
                        }
                    }

                    training_ok = true;
                } catch (const std::exception &e) {
                    std::cerr << "\n[ERROR] training failed at group " << g << ": " << e.what() << "\n";
                }

                if (!training_ok) {
                    Cursor = precursor;
                    std::cerr << "[cursor] rolled back to trained=" << precursor.total_seen << "\n";
                }

                if (n_examples >= RL_K) {
                    auto [rl_nll_r, rl_acc_r] = RL_Update(n_examples, chunk, ss_rng);
                    rl_reward_acc += rl_nll_r;
                    rl_acc_acc += rl_acc_r;

                    rl_reward_count++;
                }

                std::cout << "\033[2m  [g" << g + 1 << "/" << Groups << "] done  "
                        << "loss=" << group_loss / n_batches
                        << "  trained=" << Cursor.total_seen << "\033[0m\n";
            }
            Network.SaveForTraining(checkpoint_model);
            RL_State.Save();
            Cursor.Save();
            std::cout << "[save] session end: model + rl_state written\n";
        }
    };
}


// ======================================================================
// FILE: main.cpp
// ======================================================================

#include "src/TTTN.hpp"

using namespace TTTN;


int main() {
    using BPEType = BytePairTokenizer<8192>;
    BPEType bpe;

    // ---- FIT ----
    std::puts("=== Fitting BPE on corpus ===");
    bpe.BPE("tttn_dump.txt", "corpus_tokenized.bin");
    bpe.Save("bpe_model.bin");
    std::puts("Model saved to bpe_model.bin\n");

    // ---- PRINT MAP ----
    std::puts("=== Token Map ===");
    bpe.PrintMap();
    std::putchar('\n');

    // ---- TOKENIZE A TEXT FILE ----
    std::puts("=== Tokenizing text.txt ===");
    BPEType::TextToWords("oldmain.txt", "text_words.bin");
    auto tokens = bpe.Tokenize("text_words.bin");

    std::puts("--- Token sequence ---");
    for (const uint16_t tok: tokens) {
        const auto &entry = bpe.GetMap()[tok];
        std::string display;
        for (uint8_t i = 0; i < entry.len; ++i) {
            uint8_t b = entry.bytes[i];
            if (b >= 32 && b < 127) display += static_cast<char>(b);
            else display += "[" + std::to_string(b) + "]";
        }
        std::printf("%5u : %s\n", tok, display.c_str());
    }

    // ---- DETOKENIZE ----
    std::putchar('\n');
    std::puts("=== Detokenized output ===");
    std::string reconstructed = bpe.Detokenize(tokens);
    std::puts(reconstructed.c_str());

    // ---- RELOAD AND VERIFY ----
    std::putchar('\n');
    std::puts("=== Reload from disk and re-detokenize ===");
    BPEType bpe2;
    bpe2.Load("bpe_model.bin");
    std::printf("Loaded MapLen=%u MergeOrder.size=%zu\n", bpe2.GetMapLen(), bpe2.GetMergeOrder().size());

    auto tokens2 = bpe2.Tokenize("text_words.bin");
    std::string reconstructed2 = bpe2.Detokenize(tokens2);
    std::puts(reconstructed2 == reconstructed ? "MATCH" : "MISMATCH");

    return 0;
}


// ======================================================================
// FILE: scripts/sync_docs.py
// ======================================================================

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
sync_docs.py

README is the documentation source of truth.
Anchor: // @doc: <signature>  placed manually in .hpp files.

Algorithm per file:
  1. Strip all generated /** */ blocks immediately following // @doc: lines
  2. Deduplicate repeated // @doc: lines with the same signature (keeps last)
  3. Match each sentinel to a README entry by normalized signature
  4. Insert a fresh /** */ doc block immediately after each matched sentinel
  5. Report mismatches in both directions:
       (a) // @doc: sentinels with no README entry
       (b) README entries whose target file has no matching sentinel
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import re
import sys
from collections import defaultdict
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path

SENTINEL = "// @doc:"


# ── Data types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ReadmeEntry:
    signature: str
    relpath: str
    bullets: list[str]


@dataclass
class Sentinel:
    line_idx: int   # index in the stripped lines list
    signature: str
    key: str        # normalize(signature)


# ── Normalization ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def normalize(s: str) -> str:
    """Collapse all whitespace, drop storage qualifiers, canonicalize punctuation."""
    s = re.sub(r"/\*.*?\*/", " ", s, flags=re.DOTALL)
    s = re.sub(r"//.*$", " ", s, flags=re.MULTILINE)
    s = re.sub(
        r"\b(static|constexpr|inline|virtual|explicit|friend|extern"
        r"|consteval|constinit|mutable|override|final)\b",
        " ", s,
    )
    for pat, repl in (
        (r"\s*<\s*", "<"), (r"\s*>\s*", ">"),
        (r"\s*\(\s*", "("), (r"\s*\)\s*", ")"),
        (r"\s*,\s*", ","), (r"\s*&\s*", "&"),
        (r"\s*\*\s*", "*"), (r"\s*=\s*", "="),
        (r"\s*::\s*", "::"),
    ):
        s = re.sub(pat, repl, s)
    return re.sub(r"\s+", "", s).strip()


# ── README parsing ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

_INLINE_RE      = re.compile(r"\[`([^`]+)`\]\(([^)]+)\)")
_BLOCK_START_RE = re.compile(r"^\s*-\s+.*\[\s*$")
_BLOCK_BODY_RE  = re.compile(r"^\s*`([^`]+)`\]\(([^)]+)\)")
_STOP_RE        = re.compile(r"^\s*(#{1,6}\s|---+\s*$)")
_BULLET_RE      = re.compile(r"^\s*-\s+(.+?)\s*$")


def parse_readme(readme_path: Path) -> list[ReadmeEntry]:
    """
    Extract all entries with a [`sig`](path) link plus following bullets.
    Handles both inline form:  - Name — [`sig`](path)
    and block (two-line) form:  - Name — [
                                    `sig`](path)
    Only entries with at least one non-empty bullet are returned.
    """
    lines = readme_path.read_text().splitlines()
    out: list[ReadmeEntry] = []
    i = 0
    while i < len(lines):
        sig: str | None = None
        relpath: str | None = None
        j: int = 0

        m = _INLINE_RE.search(lines[i])
        if m:
            sig, relpath, j = m.group(1).strip(), m.group(2).strip(), i + 1
        elif _BLOCK_START_RE.match(lines[i]):
            k = i + 1
            while k < len(lines) and not lines[k].strip():
                k += 1
            if k < len(lines):
                m2 = _BLOCK_BODY_RE.match(lines[k])
                if m2:
                    sig, relpath, j = m2.group(1).strip(), m2.group(2).strip(), k + 1

        if sig is None:
            i += 1
            continue

        bullets: list[str] = []
        current: str | None = None
        while j < len(lines):
            dl = lines[j]
            # Stop at section headers, another entry (inline or block), or blank line
            if _STOP_RE.match(dl) or _INLINE_RE.search(dl) or _BLOCK_START_RE.match(dl):
                break
            bm = _BULLET_RE.match(dl)
            if bm:
                if current is not None:
                    bullets.append(current)
                current = bm.group(1).strip()
            elif current is not None and dl.strip():
                current += " " + dl.strip()
            elif not dl.strip():
                break
            j += 1
        if current is not None:
            bullets.append(current)
        if bullets:
            out.append(ReadmeEntry(sig, relpath, bullets))
        i += 1
    return out


# ── Strip & dedup ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def strip_and_dedup(lines: list[str]) -> list[str]:
    """
    Pass 1 — remove every generated /** */ block that immediately follows a
              // @doc: line (handles single-line and multi-line forms).
    Pass 2 — collapse runs of identical consecutive // @doc: lines to one.
    """
    # Pass 1: strip generated doc blocks
    out: list[str] = []
    i = 0
    while i < len(lines):
        if lines[i].lstrip().startswith(SENTINEL):
            out.append(lines[i])
            i += 1
            # Remove all consecutive generated doc blocks
            while i < len(lines):
                s = lines[i].strip()
                if s.startswith("/**") and s.endswith("*/"):
                    i += 1  # single-line /** ... */
                elif s == "/**":
                    i += 1
                    while i < len(lines) and lines[i].strip() != "*/":
                        i += 1
                    if i < len(lines):
                        i += 1  # consume */
                else:
                    break
        else:
            out.append(lines[i])
            i += 1

    # Pass 2: collapse duplicate consecutive // @doc: lines (same sig, keep last)
    result: list[str] = []
    i = 0
    while i < len(out):
        if out[i].lstrip().startswith(SENTINEL):
            sig = out[i].lstrip()[len(SENTINEL):].strip()
            # Advance past all consecutive duplicates with the same sig
            j = i + 1
            while j < len(out) and out[j].lstrip().startswith(SENTINEL):
                next_sig = out[j].lstrip()[len(SENTINEL):].strip()
                if next_sig == sig:
                    j += 1
                else:
                    break
            # Keep the last one of this run
            result.append(out[j - 1])
            i = j
        else:
            result.append(out[i])
            i += 1
    return result


# ── Sentinel extraction ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def find_sentinels(lines: list[str]) -> list[Sentinel]:
    out: list[Sentinel] = []
    for i, line in enumerate(lines):
        s = line.lstrip()
        if not s.startswith(SENTINEL):
            continue
        sig = s[len(SENTINEL):].strip()
        if sig:
            out.append(Sentinel(i, sig, normalize(sig)))
    return out


# ── Doc block generation ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def doc_block(bullets: list[str], indent: int, sig: str) -> list[str]:
    pad = " " * indent
    if len(bullets) == 1:
        return [f"{pad}/** {bullets[0]} */"]
    block = [f"{pad}/**"]
    for b in bullets:
        block.append(f"{pad} * {b}")
    block.append(f"{pad} */")
    return block


# ── Matching ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def match_entry(key: str, sig: str, by_key: dict[str, ReadmeEntry]) -> ReadmeEntry | None:
    if key in by_key:
        return by_key[key]

    # Containment fallback
    candidates = [e for k, e in by_key.items() if key in k or k in key]
    if len(candidates) == 1:
        return candidates[0]
    if len(candidates) > 1:
        return min(candidates, key=lambda e: abs(len(normalize(e.signature)) - len(key)))

    # Symbol-name fallback: match on the last identifier token
    toks = re.findall(r"[A-Za-z_]\w*", sig)
    if toks:
        name = toks[-1]
        by_name = [e for k, e in by_key.items() if name in k]
        if len(by_name) == 1:
            return by_name[0]
        if len(by_name) > 1:
            return min(by_name, key=lambda e: abs(len(normalize(e.signature)) - len(key)))

    return None


# ── Per-file sync ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def sync_file(
    filepath: Path,
    entries: list[ReadmeEntry],
) -> tuple[list[str], list[str]]:
    """
    Sync one file. Returns:
      sentinel_unmatched: sentinel sigs that had no README entry
      readme_unmatched:   README entry sigs that had no sentinel match
    Writes the updated file in place.
    """
    lines = strip_and_dedup(filepath.read_text().splitlines())
    sentinels = find_sentinels(lines)
    by_key = {normalize(e.signature): e for e in entries}

    matched_readme_keys: set[str] = set()
    sentinel_unmatched: list[str] = []
    inserts: list[tuple[int, list[str]]] = []  # (insert_position, block_lines)

    for sent in sentinels:
        entry = match_entry(sent.key, sent.signature, by_key)
        if entry is None:
            sentinel_unmatched.append(sent.signature)
            continue
        matched_readme_keys.add(normalize(entry.signature))
        indent = len(lines[sent.line_idx]) - len(lines[sent.line_idx].lstrip())
        inserts.append((sent.line_idx + 1, doc_block(entry.bullets, indent, entry.signature)))

    # Insert from bottom up so earlier indices stay valid
    inserts.sort(key=lambda t: t[0], reverse=True)
    for pos, block in inserts:
        lines[pos:pos] = block

    filepath.write_text("\n".join(lines) + "\n")

    readme_unmatched = [
        e.signature for e in entries
        if normalize(e.signature) not in matched_readme_keys
    ]
    return sentinel_unmatched, readme_unmatched


# ── Entry point ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

def main() -> None:
    readme_path = Path(sys.argv[1]) if len(sys.argv) > 1 else Path("README.md")
    if not readme_path.exists():
        print(f"ERROR: README not found: {readme_path}")
        raise SystemExit(1)

    base = readme_path.parent
    entries = parse_readme(readme_path)
    print(f"Found {len(entries)} documented README entries")

    by_file: dict[Path, list[ReadmeEntry]] = defaultdict(list)
    for e in entries:
        by_file[(base / e.relpath).resolve()].append(e)

    total_sentinel_unmatched = 0
    total_readme_unmatched = 0

    for filepath, items in sorted(by_file.items(), key=lambda kv: str(kv[0])):
        rel = filepath.relative_to(base.resolve()) if filepath.exists() else filepath
        if not filepath.exists():
            print(f"\nSKIP {rel}: file not found")
            continue

        print(f"\nSync {rel}  ({len(items)} README entries)")
        sentinel_unmatched, readme_unmatched = sync_file(filepath, items)

        if sentinel_unmatched:
            print("  Sentinels with no README entry:")
            for s in sentinel_unmatched:
                print(f"    @doc: {s}")
            total_sentinel_unmatched += len(sentinel_unmatched)
        else:
            print("  Sentinels with no README entry: none")

        if readme_unmatched:
            print("  README entries with no sentinel:")
            for s in readme_unmatched:
                print(f"    readme: {s}")
            total_readme_unmatched += len(readme_unmatched)
        else:
            print("  README entries with no sentinel: none")

    print("\nSummary")
    print(f"  Sentinels with no README entry:  {total_sentinel_unmatched}")
    print(f"  README entries with no sentinel: {total_readme_unmatched}")
    if total_sentinel_unmatched or total_readme_unmatched:
        print("  Sync finished with mismatches (see above).")
    else:
        print("  Sync complete — full bidirectional coverage.")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


// ======================================================================
// FILE: scripts/dump_lib.py
// ======================================================================

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""dump_lib.py — concatenate the full TTTN library into one text file.

Writes every .hpp file in src/ (except pstld.h) in alphabetical order,
then main.cpp, then the Python scripts.
Output: tttn_dump.txt
"""

from pathlib import Path

SCRIPT_DIR = Path(__file__).parent.parent.resolve()
SRC_DIR = SCRIPT_DIR / "src"
OUTPUT = SCRIPT_DIR / "tttn_dump.txt"


def dump(out, path: Path) -> None:
    label = str(path.relative_to(SCRIPT_DIR))
    out.write(f"// {'='*70}\n")
    out.write(f"// FILE: {label}\n")
    out.write(f"// {'='*70}\n\n")
    out.write(path.read_text())
    out.write("\n\n")


def main() -> None:
    src_files = sorted(
        p for p in SRC_DIR.iterdir()
        if p.suffix in (".hpp", ".h") and p.name != "pstld.h"
    )

    written: list[Path] = []
    with OUTPUT.open("w") as out:
        for f in src_files:
            dump(out, f)
            written.append(f)

        main_cpp = SCRIPT_DIR / "main.cpp"
        if main_cpp.exists():
            dump(out, main_cpp)
            written.append(main_cpp)

        for script in ("scripts/sync_docs.py", "scripts/dump_lib.py", "scripts/generate_brackets.py"):
            p = SCRIPT_DIR / script
            if p.exists():
                dump(out, p)
                written.append(p)

    total_lines = sum(1 for _ in OUTPUT.open())
    print(f"==> Dumped {len(written)} files -> {OUTPUT}  ({total_lines} lines)")
    for p in written:
        print(f"    {p.relative_to(SCRIPT_DIR)}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


// ======================================================================
// FILE: scripts/generate_brackets.py
// ======================================================================

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""generate_brackets.py — bracket/brace/paren sequence classifier dataset.

Sequences are exactly SEQ_LEN=32 chars, padded with blank tokens.
Label 1 = all brackets properly closed.  Label 0 = invalid.
CSV format: label, t0, t1, ..., t31   (token indices 0-6)

Token vocabulary:
  0 = (   1 = )   2 = [   3 = ]   4 = {   5 = }   6 = blank
"""

import random, csv

SEQ_LEN = 32
OPEN  = '([{'
CLOSE = ')]}'
PAIR  = {'(':')', '[':']', '{':'}'}
MATCH = {')':'(', ']':'[', '}':'{'}
BLANK = ' '
VOCAB = ['(', ')', '[', ']', '{', '}', ' ']
TOK   = {c: i for i, c in enumerate(VOCAB)}


def is_valid(tokens):
    stk = []
    for c in tokens:
        if c == BLANK:
            continue
        if c in OPEN:
            stk.append(c)
        elif c in CLOSE:
            if not stk or stk[-1] != MATCH[c]:
                return False
            stk.pop()
    return not stk


def gen_valid(rng, min_len=2, max_len=26, max_depth=5):
    """Build a random valid bracket sequence, then pad to SEQ_LEN."""
    tokens = []
    stack  = []
    target_len = rng.randint(min_len, max_len)

    while len(tokens) < target_len:
        remaining = target_len - len(tokens)
        must_close = len(stack)

        if must_close >= remaining:
            # No room to open — close everything
            tokens.append(PAIR[stack.pop()])
        elif stack and rng.random() < 0.45:
            # Close current group
            tokens.append(PAIR[stack.pop()])
        elif len(stack) < max_depth and remaining > must_close + 1 and rng.random() < 0.55:
            # Open a new group
            ch = rng.choice(OPEN)
            tokens.append(ch)
            stack.append(ch)
        # else: stay idle (can happen when depth limit hit)

    # Force-close any remaining open groups
    while stack:
        tokens.append(PAIR[stack.pop()])

    # Pad with blanks
    tokens += [BLANK] * (SEQ_LEN - len(tokens))
    return tokens[:SEQ_LEN]


def gen_invalid(rng, max_attempts=10):
    """Corrupt a valid sequence.  Returns a guaranteed-invalid token list."""
    for _ in range(max_attempts):
        base = gen_valid(rng)
        s    = base[:]

        non_blank = [i for i, c in enumerate(s) if c != BLANK]
        if not non_blank:
            continue

        mode = rng.randint(0, 3)
        i    = rng.choice(non_blank)

        if mode == 0:
            # Replace a bracket with a different one (often wrong type)
            others = [c for c in '()[]{}' if c != s[i]]
            s[i] = rng.choice(others)
        elif mode == 1:
            # Delete one bracket (replace with blank)
            s[i] = BLANK
        elif mode == 2 and len(non_blank) >= 2:
            # Swap two bracket positions
            j = rng.choice([x for x in non_blank if x != i])
            s[i], s[j] = s[j], s[i]
        else:
            # Insert an extra closing bracket somewhere
            s[i] = rng.choice(CLOSE)

        if not is_valid(s):
            return s

    # Fallback: brute-force random sequence that happens to be invalid
    while True:
        s = rng.choices(VOCAB, weights=[2, 2, 2, 2, 2, 2, 6], k=SEQ_LEN)
        if not is_valid(s):
            return s


def write_csv(path, n, rng):
    import time
    counts = [0, 0]
    rows   = []
    i      = 0
    t0 = time.time()
    while i < n:
        want_valid = (i % 2 == 0)
        if want_valid:
            s   = gen_valid(rng)
            lbl = 1
        else:
            s   = gen_invalid(rng)
            lbl = 0

        # Sanity-check (generator bugs would produce wrong labels)
        if bool(is_valid(s)) != bool(lbl):
            continue

        rows.append([lbl] + [TOK[c] for c in s])
        counts[lbl] += 1
        i += 1

        if i % 1000 == 0:
            elapsed = time.time() - t0
            rate = i / elapsed if elapsed > 0 else 0
            eta  = (n - i) / rate if rate > 0 else 0
            print(f"  {path}: {i}/{n}  ({rate:.0f}/s  ETA {eta:.1f}s)", end='\r', flush=True)

    print()  # newline after progress line
    with open(path, 'w', newline='') as f:
        w = csv.writer(f)
        w.writerow(['label'] + [f't{j}' for j in range(SEQ_LEN)])
        w.writerows(rows)

    print(f"  {path}: {n} samples  (valid={counts[1]}, invalid={counts[0]})")


if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("Generating bracket datasets...")
    write_csv('data/brackets_train.csv', 10000, random.Random(42))
    write_csv('data/brackets_test.csv',   1000, random.Random(123))
    print("Done.")
